  63 | @dataclass
  64 | class _SingleEquationState:
  65 |     calls: int = 0
  66 |     template_fingerprint: str | None = None
  67 |     result_snapshot: dict[str, Any] | None = None
  68 | 
  69 | 
  70 | _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE = threading.local()
  71 | 
  72 | 
  73 | @contextmanager
  74 | def single_equation_evaluation():
  75 |     """
  76 |     Enforce the benchmark contract for one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call.
  77 | 
  78 |     A candidate may build helper subexpressions, but it may submit exactly one
  79 |     symbolic template to the scorer. This prevents reward hacking where a
  80 |     program tries many equations and returns whichever receives the best score.
  81 |     """
  82 |     previous = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
  83 |     state = _SingleEquationState()
  84 |     _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = state
  85 |     try:
  86 |         yield
  87 |         if state.calls != 1:
  88 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
  89 |                 "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must call "
  90 |                 "evaluate_expression() exactly once with one symbolic equation template. "
  91 |                 f"It submitted {state.calls} templates. Build one base equation and let "
  92 |                 "the harness fit that equation's constants per dataset."
  93 |             )
  94 |     finally:
  95 |         _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = previous
  96 | 
  97 | 
  98 | def _record_scored_template(template: sp.Expr) -> None:
  99 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 100 |     if state is None:
 101 |         return
 102 | 
 103 |     state.calls += 1
 104 |     fingerprint = sp.srepr(template)
 105 |     if state.template_fingerprint is None:
 106 |         state.template_fingerprint = fingerprint
 107 |         return
 108 | 
 109 |     if state.template_fingerprint != fingerprint:
 110 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 111 |             "Single-equation violation: one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call "
 112 |             "submitted multiple different symbolic equation templates. The base "
 113 |             "equation must be fixed; only fitted constants may change."
 114 |         )
 115 | 
 116 |     raise SingleEquationViolation(
 117 |         "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() called "
 118 |         "evaluate_expression()/fit_expression_constants() more than once. Do not "
 119 |         "try multiple equation templates or multiple scorer calls and pick the "
 120 |         "best result; submit exactly one symbolic expression."
 121 |     )
 122 | 
 123 | 
 124 | def _record_scorer_result(result: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
 125 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 126 |     if state is not None:
 127 |         state.result_snapshot = copy.deepcopy(result)
 128 | 
 129 | 
 130 | def validate_single_equation_result(result: Any) -> None:
 131 |     """
 132 |     Ensure the candidate returns the actual scorer output, unchanged.
 133 | 
 134 |     This closes the loophole where a program calls evaluate_expression() once
 135 |     to satisfy the call-count guard, then fabricates or edits the metrics it
 136 |     returns to the evaluator.
 137 |     """
 138 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 139 |     if state is None:
 140 |         return
 141 | 
 142 |     if state.result_snapshot is None:
 143 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 144 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "
 145 |             "the dictionary produced by evaluate_expression()."
 146 |         )
 147 | 
 148 |     if result != state.result_snapshot:
 149 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 150 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "
 151 |             "the exact, unmodified result from its single evaluate_expression() "
 152 |             "call. Do not fabricate, overwrite, wrap, or post-process metrics."
 153 |         )

 200 | def _validate_expression_template(template: sp.Expr, constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol]) -> None:
 201 |     complexity = int(_complexity(template))
 202 |     if complexity > MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY:
 203 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 204 |             "Single-equation violation: symbolic template is too complex "
 205 |             f"({complexity} nodes > limit {MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY}). Do not hide "
 206 |             "many candidate equations inside one oversized expression."
 207 |         )
 208 | 
 209 |     if len(constants) > MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS:
 210 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 211 |             "Single-equation violation: too many fitted constants "
 212 |             f"({len(constants)} > limit {MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS}). Use one compact "
 213 |             "universal equation, not an over-parameterized surrogate."
 214 |         )
 215 | 
 216 |     for node in sp.preorder_traversal(template):
 217 |         if isinstance(node, _BANNED_EXPR_TYPES) or node.func.__name__ in _BANNED_EXPR_FUNCTIONS:
 218 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
 219 |                 "Single-equation violation: conditional, piecewise, discontinuous, "
 220 |                 f"or gated symbolic construct '{node.func.__name__}' is not allowed. "
 221 |                 "Use one smooth global equation template."

 225 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:

 227 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
 228 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 229 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
 230 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
 231 |         else:
 232 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
 233 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)

 791 | ) -> np.ndarray:
 792 |     """Integrate dc/dt=f(t, m0, M0, c) per cleaned X/Y curve."""
 793 |     import warnings
 794 | 
 795 |     from scipy.integrate import odeint
 796 | 
 797 |     X = np.asarray(X, dtype=float)
 798 |     y_known = np.asarray(y_known, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 799 |     theta = np.asarray(theta, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 800 |     predictions = np.full_like(y_known, np.nan, dtype=float)
 801 | 
 802 |     for curve_idx in _curve_indices(X):
 803 |         ordered_idx = curve_idx[np.argsort(X[curve_idx, 0])]
 804 |         times = X[ordered_idx, 0]
 805 |         observed = y_known[ordered_idx]
 806 |         static_features = [float(value) for value in X[ordered_idx[0], 1:-1]]
 807 | 
 808 |         if len(ordered_idx) == 1 or float(times[-1] - times[0]) <= 0.0:
 809 |             predictions[ordered_idx] = observed[0]
 810 |             continue
 811 | 
 812 |         def dc_dt(c_state: np.ndarray, time_value: float) -> float:
 813 |             c_value = float(np.asarray(c_state, dtype=float).reshape(-1)[0])
 814 |             value = rhs_fn(float(time_value), *static_features, c_value, *theta)
 815 |             value = float(np.asarray(value, dtype=float).reshape(-1)[0])
 816 |             if not np.isfinite(value):
 817 |                 raise FloatingPointError("non-finite ODE derivative")
 818 |             return value
 819 | 
 820 |         with warnings.catch_warnings():
 821 |             warnings.simplefilter("ignore")
 822 |             integrated = odeint(
 823 |                 dc_dt,
 824 |                 float(observed[0]),
 825 |                 times,
 826 |                 mxstep=1000,
 827 |             )
 828 |         curve_pred = np.asarray(integrated, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 829 |         if curve_pred.shape != observed.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(curve_pred)):

 726 | def _curve_shape_loss(X: np.ndarray, y_true: np.ndarray, y_pred: np.ndarray) -> float:
 727 |     """Bounded shape mismatch based on curve slopes and half-response timing."""
 728 |     X = np.asarray(X, dtype=float)
 729 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 730 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 731 |     if X.shape[0] != y_true.size or y_true.shape != y_pred.shape or y_true.size < 3:
 732 |         return 0.0
 733 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
 734 |         return 1.0
 735 | 
 736 |     curve_ids = _ARRAY_CURVE_IDS.get(id(X))
 737 |     if curve_ids is None or curve_ids.shape[0] != X.shape[0]:
 738 |         curve_ids = np.zeros(X.shape[0], dtype=int)
 739 | 
 740 |     curve_losses: list[float] = []
 741 |     for curve_id in dict.fromkeys(np.asarray(curve_ids, dtype=int)):
 742 |         idx = np.flatnonzero(curve_ids == curve_id)
 743 |         if idx.size < 3:
 744 |             continue
 745 |         order = idx[np.argsort(X[idx, 0])]
 746 |         x = X[order, 0]
 747 |         true_curve = y_true[order]
 748 |         pred_curve = y_pred[order]
 749 |         dx = np.diff(x)
 750 |         valid_dx = np.abs(dx) > 1e-12
 751 |         if not np.any(valid_dx):
 752 |             continue
 753 |         true_slope = np.diff(true_curve)[valid_dx] / dx[valid_dx]
 754 |         pred_slope = np.diff(pred_curve)[valid_dx] / dx[valid_dx]
 755 |         slope_scale = float(np.mean(true_slope**2))
 756 |         slope_raw = float(np.mean((pred_slope - true_slope) ** 2))
 757 |         slope_loss = (
 758 |             _bounded_loss(slope_raw / slope_scale)
 759 |             if slope_scale > 0.0
 760 |             else _bounded_loss(slope_raw)
 761 |         )
 762 | 
 763 |         true_half = _half_response_time(x, true_curve)
 764 |         pred_half = _half_response_time(x, pred_curve)
 765 |         if true_half is None and pred_half is None:
 766 |             timing_loss = 0.0
 767 |         elif true_half is None or pred_half is None:
 768 |             timing_loss = 1.0
 769 |         else:
 770 |             timing_loss = min(abs(float(pred_half) - float(true_half)), 1.0)
 771 | 
 772 |         curve_losses.append(0.7 * slope_loss + 0.3 * timing_loss)
 773 | 
 774 |     if not curve_losses:
 775 |         return 0.0
 776 |     return float(np.mean(curve_losses))
 777 |

 781 |         return float("inf")

 783 |     return float((1.0 - SHAPE_LOSS_WEIGHT) * float(nmse_val) + SHAPE_LOSS_WEIGHT * bounded_shape)

  70 | _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE = threading.local()

  73 | @contextmanager
  74 | def single_equation_evaluation():
  75 |     """
  76 |     Enforce the benchmark contract for one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call.
  77 | 
  78 |     A candidate may build helper subexpressions, but it may submit exactly one
  79 |     symbolic template to the scorer. This prevents reward hacking where a
  80 |     program tries many equations and returns whichever receives the best score.
  81 |     """
  82 |     previous = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
  83 |     state = _SingleEquationState()
  84 |     _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = state
  85 |     try:
  86 |         yield
  87 |         if state.calls != 1:
  88 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
  89 |                 "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must call "
  90 |                 "evaluate_expression() exactly once with one symbolic equation template. "
  91 |                 f"It submitted {state.calls} templates. Build one base equation and let "
  92 |                 "the harness fit that equation's constants per dataset."
  93 |             )
  94 |     finally:
  95 |         _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = previous
  96 | 
  97 | 
  98 | def _record_scored_template(template: sp.Expr) -> None:
  99 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 100 |     if state is None:
 101 |         return
 102 | 
 103 |     state.calls += 1
 104 |     fingerprint = sp.srepr(template)
 105 |     if state.template_fingerprint is None:
 106 |         state.template_fingerprint = fingerprint
 107 |         return
 108 | 
 109 |     if state.template_fingerprint != fingerprint:
 110 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 111 |             "Single-equation violation: one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call "

 629 | def _parsimony_penalty_factor(complexity: float) -> float:
 630 |     """Bounded penalty factor for expression complexity."""
 631 |     if not np.isfinite(complexity) or PARSIMONY_COMPLEXITY_SCALE <= 0:
 632 |         return 1.0
 633 |     normalized = min(max(float(complexity), 0.0) / PARSIMONY_COMPLEXITY_SCALE, 1.0)
 634 |     return max(0.0, 1.0 - PARSIMONY_WEIGHT * normalized)

 637 | def _gaussian_smooth_1d(values: np.ndarray, sigma: float = GAUSSIAN_SMOOTH_SIGMA) -> np.ndarray:
 638 |     values = np.asarray(values, dtype=float).ravel()
 639 |     if values.size < 3 or sigma <= 0.0:
 640 |         return values
 641 |     radius = max(1, int(round(3.0 * sigma)))
 642 |     offsets = np.arange(-radius, radius + 1, dtype=float)
 643 |     kernel = np.exp(-0.5 * (offsets / sigma) ** 2)
 644 |     kernel /= np.sum(kernel)
 645 |     padded = np.pad(values, (radius, radius), mode="edge")
 646 |     return np.convolve(padded, kernel, mode="valid")
